When Intel Wireless-AC 9260 cards with these PCI subdevice IDs are enumerated, the driver cannot find a matching entry in the device info table and falls back to the catch-all PCI device ID entry with `PCI_ANY_ID`. This causes the device to be configured with the generic `iwl9000_trans_cfg` configuration instead of the correct `iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg` configuration, resulting in firmware loading failures.\n\n**Impact:** Firmware loading failures for Intel Wireless-AC 9260 cards with these specific OEM variants.\n\nThe fault localization result has been written to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` with 95% confidence.\n\n**Sources:**\n- [Linux Kernel Bug 206661 - iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526](https://bugzilla.kernel.org/show_bug.cgi?id=206661)\n- [Ubuntu Bug Report on iwlwifi Intel 9260](https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/linux/+bug/1871430)","stop_reason":null,"session_id":"f6b85b78-ab5d-4b8e-8563-a242f3c922df","total_cost_usd":0.30927165,"usage":{"input_tokens":232,"cache_creation_input_tokens":59753,"cache_read_input_tokens":1701824,"output_tokens":11756,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":59753,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001":{"inputTokens":5148,"outputTokens":11850,"cacheReadInputTokens":1701824,"cacheCreationInputTokens":59753,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":0.30927165,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"fast_mode_state":"off","uuid":"33c2cf81-852c-4453-8fa5-3aa22cc3cca3"}
